<div id="review_1958694016" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1958694016" />
    <a title="Jiana" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10502567-jiana"><img alt="Jiana" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1540380229p2/10502567.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1958694016?book_show_action=true">Apr 09, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jiana" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jiana" href="/user/show/10502567-jiana">Jiana</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780062396624" href="/book/show/26072584-ruined">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1958694016" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17863571968114386340"><b>2.5</b><br/><br/>Buddy read with <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/49148508' rel='nofollow noopener'>Tweety</a>!!<br/><br/><b>One word to describe Ruined: Boring</b><br/><br/>I was literally bored the entire time I was reading this. I couldn't connect to any of the characters (except Cas, he's a cutie) and the plot. I just wasn't invested at all. I sat there reading and just wanting it to end. I hate DNFing books and I always have hopes they'll pick up, but unfortunately Ruined didn't pick up. I'm probably a minority because a lot of reviews I read were praising how fast it was. Who knows. Might be because</span>
  <span id="freeText17863571968114386340" style="display:none"><b>2.5</b><br /><br />Buddy read with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/49148508" rel="nofollow noopener">Tweety</a>!!<br /><br /><b>One word to describe Ruined: Boring</b><br /><br />I was literally bored the entire time I was reading this. I couldn't connect to any of the characters (except Cas, he's a cutie) and the plot. I just wasn't invested at all. I sat there reading and just wanting it to end. I hate DNFing books and I always have hopes they'll pick up, but unfortunately Ruined didn't pick up. I'm probably a minority because a lot of reviews I read were praising how fast it was. Who knows. Might be because of my damn slump. But basically, I was going to cry at how boring it was.<br /><br />Ruined offered nothing new to YA genre, but I didn't really care about that. When you read too many books, you always get to a point where books are somewhat repetitive. Also, there's more to a book than its plot. There's the writing, the characters, the pacing, the execution... <br /><br />--&gt; Writing: Pretty simplistic and easy to follow, despite being a tad confused at first with the world building. (too many names!)<br />--&gt; Characters: Like I stated before, I couldn't connect to any of them except Cas. I just didn't care. Cas was adorable and he's basically one of two reasons I didn't rate this lower. Our MC, Em was indeed a badass, but I also couldn't care less. I liked the relationship between Cas and Em, there was angst and insta-love. Again, as I have stated many times before in many of my reviews: I don't mind insta-love if it isn't over the top. Cas and Em's wasn't really extreme, but I was hoping it took a little more longer to develop.<br />--&gt; Pacing: Like I said before, boring.<br />--&gt; Execution: Good despite not having anything special or new. <br /><br />I'm still going to read the second book when it comes out because I think it has the potential to become really good. I'm curious to see where things will go.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17863571968114386340" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer2202622256070107135"><b>THE REVIEW</b><br/><br/><b>Why this book?</b><br/>This sounded awesome<br/><br/><b>What I thought</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458674452ra/18517443.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This book was amazing it was full of action, love and loyalty. Em is a kick ass heroine who is ready for revenge. I absolutely loved Cas he has a beautiful heart and doesn’t believe what his father is doing is right.   <span id="freeText2202622256070107135" style="display:none"><b>THE REVIEW</b><br><br><b>Why this book?</b><br>This sounded awesome<br><br><b>What I thought</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458674452ra/18517443.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book was amazing it was full of action, love and loyalty. <span id="freeTextContainer15771584069046031811">I loved Amy's other series, so I was beyond excited to see what her new book was going to be about. Oh man, I was woefully unprepared for the amount of awesome.<br/><br/>Em is an awesome MC.   <span id="freeText15771584069046031811" style="display:none">I loved Amy's other series, so I was beyond excited to see what her new book was going to be about. Oh man, I was woefully unprepared for the amount of awesome.<br /><br />Em is an awesome MC. She doesn't have magic, and while that's seen as a disadvantage in her kingdom, she puts together quite a plan. Of course things don't necessarily turn out the way she planned and how it plays out is fabulous.<br /><br />Cas is lovely and I really enjoyed being able to see his side of everything. There are a lot of other excellent characters and Amy had a way of making me like the characters I hate too.<br /><br />I truly love how Amy creates kick ass heroines and Em is no exception. This book is filled with action, swoons, double crossings, and one hell of an ending. I can't even wait to see what happens next.<br /><br />**Huge thanks to Harper Teen and Edelweiss for providing the arc in exchange for an honest review**<br /><br />**Squishy hugs to Amy for sending me a physical arc**</span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1207792518" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1207792518" />
    <a title="Alyssa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8472395-alyssa"><img alt="Alyssa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1500935920p2/8472395.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1207792518?book_show_action=true">Feb 21, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alyssa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alyssa" href="/user/show/8472395-alyssa">Alyssa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8472395-alyssa?shelf=2016-releases">2016-releases</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1207792518" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14940176898422700032">OMGGGGGGGGGGGGGGGGGGGGGGGG!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!<br/><br/><br/>***<a href='http://eaterofbooks.blogspot.com/2016/03/review-ruined-by-amy-tintera.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Review posted on The Eater of Books! blog</a>***<br/><br/>Ruined by Amy Tintera<br/>Book One of the Ruined series<br/>Publisher: HarperTeen<br/>Publication Date: May 3, 2016<br/>Rating: 4 stars<br/>Source: eARC from Edelweiss<br/><br/>Summary (from Goodreads):<br/><br/>Emelina Flores has nothing. Her home in Ruina has been ravaged by war. She lacks the powers of her fellow Ruined. Worst of all, she witnessed her parents’ brutal murders and watched helplessly as her sister, Olivia, was kidnapped.<br/><br/>But because Em </span>
  <span id="freeText14940176898422700032" style="display:none">OMGGGGGGGGGGGGGGGGGGGGGGGG!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!<br /><br /><br />***<a href="http://eaterofbooks.blogspot.com/2016/03/review-ruined-by-amy-tintera.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Review posted on The Eater of Books! blog</a>***<br /><br />Ruined by Amy Tintera<br />Book One of the Ruined series<br />Publisher: HarperTeen<br />Publication Date: May 3, 2016<br />Rating: 4 stars<br />Source: eARC from Edelweiss<br /><br />Summary (from Goodreads):<br /><br />Emelina Flores has nothing. Her home in Ruina has been ravaged by war. She lacks the powers of her fellow Ruined. Worst of all, she witnessed her parents’ brutal murders and watched helplessly as her sister, Olivia, was kidnapped.<br /><br />But because Em has nothing, she has nothing to lose. Driven by a blind desire for revenge, Em sets off on a dangerous journey to the enemy kingdom of Lera. Somewhere within Lera’s borders, Em hopes to find Olivia. But in order to find her, Em must infiltrate the royal family.<br /><br />In a brilliant, elaborate plan of deception and murder, Em marries Prince Casimir, next in line to take Lera’s throne. If anyone in Lera discovers Em is not Casimir’s true betrothed, Em will be executed on the spot. But it’s the only way to salvage Em’s kingdom and what is left of her family.<br /><br />Em is determined to succeed, but the closer she gets to the prince, the more she questions her mission. Em’s rage-filled heart begins to soften. But with her life—and her family—on the line, love could be Em’s deadliest mistake.<br /><br />What I Liked:<br /><br />Ah! I don't even know where to start with this one. I keep going back and forth between five stars and four stars (I generally round down if I'm indecisive). Ruined was excellent! I was not expecting to like this book as much as I did. The story was fast-paced and engaging, and I was so thoroughly invested that I kept trying to read what clearly wasn't there, upon finishing!<br /><br />Em's parents are dead, her sister kidnapped, her country of Ruina destroyed. As the daughter of the king and queen and the rightful heir of the throne, Em wants revenge, and she wants her sister back. Em has always felt "useless", as she isn't one of the Ruined (she has no power, whereas the Ruined have incredible power). Her plan: kill Princess Mary of Vallos, marry Mary's fiance (the crown prince of Lera, which is Ruina's enemy), and destroy Lera from within, all the while rescuing Olivia. But Em doesn't expect to fall for Prince Casimir ("Cas"), and their mutual feelings for each other will throw everything out of balance for Em. When the time comes to strike, what will Em choose?<br /><br />This type of story is nothing new - in which a protagonist infiltrates the enemy kingdom in order to win their trust, but ends up falling in love with the crown prince/royalty. But I love the execution! Tintera did a great job of making this type of story into something fresh and unique.<br /><br />Immediately, as soon as the story started, I could tell how bloodthirsty Em is. And throughout the story, the bloodthirstiness is maintained. You can tell in how she thinks, acts, and feels, just how much of a survivor she is. She's not Ruined - she has no supernatural abilities - but she is beyond tough and strong and can take care of herself. She is intelligent, calculating, and did I already mention bloodthirsty? She is very skilled with weapons and kills easily, though not without remorse or regret. <br /><br />I like this change of pace in YA heroines: rarely do we get to see some REALLY bloodthirsty women (mostly it's just a bunch of kickbutt ladies who can work a sword but barely kill anyone - not that there is anything wrong with that). I like Em a lot, and I liked how she grew in this story. She grows into her lack of Ruined power (she's used to not having the power, but she isn't used to trying to lead the Ruined, who have no faith in her ability-less self).<br /><br />This book is written in third person, alternating POV, so we get to know Cas pretty well, and not just through Em's lens. Cas isn't a Ruined sympathizer necessarily, though he has doubts about the treatment and hunting of the Ruined. He marries Mary (who is Em - Em killed the real Mary), and at first he's aloof and uninterested... but he falls for her (and vice versa). His view on the Ruined changes, partly because of "Mary", partly because of how brutally his father treats them. Cas is entirely different from his parents, and of a different opinion on the Ruined. We first see an obedient, aloof Cas, but he grows and develops into a strong, decisive leader who stands up to his father and forms his own (intelligent) opinions. I like this Cas!<br /><br />The story is fairly fast-paced, which I really liked. Tintera spends enough time with the world-building and construction of characters and the setting, but she also moves the story along quickly. The first scene thrusts you into the story immediately, with Em meeting Mary to, ah, dispose of her. Then Em goes to Lera, she and Cas get married, and from then, we see Cas and Mary's budding romance, as well as an increasing conflict with the Ruined, and Mary's plan slowly happening.<br /><br />I felt like there were two climaxes in this book, which I also really liked. The first dealt with the reveal of Em to the royal family - this did NOT happen at the end of the book, like I expected. Cas and the royal family find out after the halfway point of the book, and Em's plans are interrupted. The second climax is Em trying to free her sister, but there are even more obstacles now. I'm skipping through a ton of important events, but my point is, where you think the book might end, it doesn't! I like that Tintera did not end the story with Em's true character being revealed. This kind of ending bugs me in trilogies!<br /><br />I'm being pretty vague about what it means to be "Ruined", but you'll understand entirely when you read the book. Tintera does a good job of revealing information, both all at once and bit by bit. You won't be left in the dark about pretty much anything!<br /><br />The romance is slow-burn and adorable! Two teenagers falling for each other under grim circumstances - I love it. They're married and they're uncertain around each other. Even though Em came to the castle with the plan of marrying Cas and then killing the entire royal family, she is unsure and nervous around Cas, and she falls for him. Like I said above, this book does NOT end how we think it might/should, in which Em is revealed; no, it ends later, and I like that Cas and Em still have time both not together and together, and truths are revealed. This makes waiting for book two much easier! Especially with such an adorable (and towards the very end - steamy) romance.<br /><br />The ending isn't an agonizing one, and I hesitate to call it a cliffhanger, but it doesn't end cheerfully and in a hopeful way. But it's not a cruel one, and in some ways, I think I saw it coming (though in other ways, not so much). I was shocked by certain parts of the ending, and so I'm definitely anxious to read book two! There is no doubt in my mind that I will be camping out in wait for the sequel.<br /><br />Overall, a novel that really took me by surprise! I really did not know much about this book before starting it (I'd had it added to my TBR shelf on Goodreads for years, so I just hit "download" when I saw it on Edelweiss, not even bothering to read the synopsis). In this case, it really worked out for me! I can't wait to read more.<br /><br />What I Did Not Like:<br /><br />Obviously I'm a bit peeved at the ending, but it is not the worst ending I've read! In fact, it's a decent one, though I'm beginning to question my sanity in starting new trilogies. These endings!<br /><br />Would I Recommend It:<br /><br />If you're a YA fantasy fan, it's worth it to read this one! I mean, I think anyone who enjoys YA might like this book. It's one of the most bloodthirsty YA books I've read! Bloodthirsty as in the heroine is super bloodthirsty. Good for her, her life has been terrible! Em's controlled rage and temperament is pretty impressive. Anyway! Read this book.<br /><br />Rating:<br /><br />4.5 stars -&gt; rounded down to 4 stars (what can I say, I'm stingy with the 5-star rating). This book was pretty much not on my radar (why has no one made a huge deal about this book to me yet?!), so I'm glad I went overboard with Harper's Summer galley drop and downloaded it! You all should do the same and experience this exciting story.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14940176898422700032" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1423510971" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1423510971" />
    <a title="Laura" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31923026-laura"><img alt="Laura" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1533734143p2/31923026.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1423510971?book_show_action=true">Oct 23, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laura" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laura" href="/user/show/31923026-laura">Laura</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31923026-laura?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31923026-laura?shelf=e-arc">e-arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31923026-laura?shelf=read-in-2016">read-in-2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31923026-laura?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1423510971" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17396889707180815459">That was exciting! I’m looking forward to where this series is going. <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/26074185.Ruined__Ruined___1_' title='Ruined (Ruined, #1) by Amy Tintera' rel='nofollow noopener'> Ruined</a> is a high-stakes YA fantasy about revenge.<br/><br/>Emelina lost everything a year ago when both her parents, the King and Queen of Ruina, were killed and her sister Olivia was kidnapped. Her country is being destroyed and her people are being killed. Now all Em wants is revenge. And she <b>will</b> get it.<br/><br/>Ruina is a country where the people have these magical powers that can be deadly. If you are a Ruined with powers, you have marks o</span>
  <span id="freeText17396889707180815459" style="display:none">That was exciting! I’m looking forward to where this series is going. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/26074185.Ruined__Ruined___1_" title="Ruined (Ruined, #1) by Amy Tintera" rel="nofollow noopener"> Ruined</a> is a high-stakes YA fantasy about revenge.<br /><br />Emelina lost everything a year ago when both her parents, the King and Queen of Ruina, were killed and her sister Olivia was kidnapped. Her country is being destroyed and her people are being killed. Now all Em wants is revenge. And she <b>will</b> get it.<br /><br />Ruina is a country where the people have these magical powers that can be deadly. If you are a Ruined with powers, you have marks on your body making it obvious. If you are a Ruined without powers, you are considered useless. Em is useless. This explains why her powerful younger sister is the rightful heir to the throne instead of herself. Also why Emelina has trained her whole life making her so badass with a sword. She is intelligent, strong, determined, and extremely skilled in a fight. She is constantly prepared in any situation always knowing the quickest way to kill the enemy and escape. It was refreshing having such a fierce heroine not afraid to kill. Yet she has a lot of layers to her as well.<br /><br />Prince Casimir is next in line to take Lera’s throne. His parents have set up an arranged marriage between Cas and the Princess of a neighboring country, Vallos. He’s not all that happy about the marriage circumstances..having his parents choose his bride to be. Cas has never met Princess Mary (neither have his parents), but he understands it’s best for the kingdom.<br /><br />In the kingdom of Lera, Em’s plan for revenge involves infiltrating the royal family to find out where her sister is. She’ll have to kill Princess Mary in order to be her, marry Prince Casimir, get close enough to learn where Olivia is being held captive, and then finally kill the entire royal family.<br /><br />With alternating POVs, from Em and Cas, it is really enlightening to get a sense of what’s going on in each of their heads. They are both strong, well-written characters.<br /><br />There’s plenty of action, a slow burn romance, great world building, some violence mixed in, and a good amount of twists. Overall, an excellent start to a series. Though there is a bit more background I hope we get later on. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/26074185.Ruined__Ruined___1_" title="Ruined (Ruined, #1) by Amy Tintera" rel="nofollow noopener"> Ruined</a> has a solid conclusion, while still leaving things open. I really love the direction it seems the story will take in the second book. Possibly darker? I wouldn’t put it past <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5768611.Amy_Tintera" title="Amy Tintera" rel="nofollow noopener"> Amy Tintera</a> to surprise us, but I’m hoping this series keeps getting darker like <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20821111.The_Young_Elites__The_Young_Elites___1_" title="The Young Elites (The Young Elites, #1) by Marie Lu" rel="nofollow noopener"> The Young Elites</a>. I will definitely be reading the sequel.<br /><br />An enjoyable start to a YA fantasy series for those who enjoy stories of revenge.<br /><br /><b>I received an ARC in exchange for an honest review via edelweiss.</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="17396889707180815459" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2510193473" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2510193473" />
    <a title="Beth" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44125660-beth"><img alt="Beth" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1600268807p2/44125660.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2510193473?book_show_action=true">Aug 28, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beth" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beth" href="/user/show/44125660-beth">Beth</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=2018-reads">2018-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=book-series">book-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=characters-i-loved">characters-i-loved</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=swoony-swoony">swoony-swoony</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=faves">faves</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2510193473" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17595821149990502542"><b>5 STARS!</b><br/><br/>Firstly I'm going to start by saying <u>not enough people talk about this book!</u> I absolutely loved everything about this. I saw this pop up on <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/36907106-alexis-theslothreader' rel='nofollow noopener'>Alexis's</a> YouTube channel, and I was very very intrigued to say the least! It starts off with Em plotting to marry a Prince called Casimir to help get her sister Olivia back who is a Ruined (someone who has magic abilities). From there we see the story progress on how to get Olivia back, relationships building and other characters step up and voice wh</span>
  <span id="freeText17595821149990502542" style="display:none"><b>5 STARS!</b><br /><br />Firstly I'm going to start by saying <u>not enough people talk about this book!</u> I absolutely loved everything about this. I saw this pop up on <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/36907106-alexis-theslothreader" rel="nofollow noopener">Alexis's</a> YouTube channel, and I was very very intrigued to say the least! It starts off with Em plotting to marry a Prince called Casimir to help get her sister Olivia back who is a Ruined (someone who has magic abilities). From there we see the story progress on how to get Olivia back, relationships building and other characters step up and voice what they truly believe in. <br /><br /><u>Characters</u><br /><br /><b>Em</b> who is from a family of Ruined who doesn't have any form of abilities but is the driving force behind getting her sister back. I honestly loved her character, it was interesting to see how her mind worked, and I was slightly amused at her thought process on how she'd kill people. At first she comes across as though she doesn't care, but the more you read on the more you see her passion and her love for her country and others who are Ruined. <br /><br /><i>Cas</i> is so precious, and I would protect him from everything and anything if I could. His character development was <u>EVERYTHING</u>, I loved him questioning things and trying to make a change. You could see the conflict that he had with lots of issues. <br /><br />What I found so <i>interesting</i> about the two characters coming together is the conflict they both had. They were both fighting for different (but kind of the same) things. One was doing it for one reason, and the other for another. Like it's so difficulty to pick a side, because there's good and bad to <u>both</u>. It was so endearing to see them actually <b>talk</b> about issues and I was instantly sold, hook line and sinker. <br /><br />Things I <b>liked?</b><br />- Hopefully I can word this correctly, but in this one book we got to see three races, like all of them were easy to identify, each had their own setting/what they wanted to do. It was so clear and easy to understand it was <u>great</u><br />- THE SARCASM WAS EVERYTHING. Look at this... <i>"My wife didn't smother me with a pillow! Must be love!"</i> I can't! <br />- The fighting, blood and gore and I loved it!<br />- Now I love a good romance <b>but this!</b> I thought my heart was sold on two characters, but make way for number three, because Cas you are now part of the elite.<br />- The world building and writing, ahhhh it was so good to be able to just dive into it and just follow it smoothly without having to back track and re-read things to get a handle on it, much appreciated to say the least<br />- Excuse my language her but <b>that mother fucking ending</b> was incredible.<br />- Plus I'm so ridiculously intrigued as what's to come and especially looking forward to seeing certain characters in all of their glory.<br />- What is that? Possible a gay captain of the guard? Well I am here for it, because Galo is everything.<br />- In fact all of the characters!<br /><br />I need to stop gushing.<br /><br />Things I <b>didn't like?</b><br />- AHAHAHAHAHAHAHAHAHAHA I liked everything I'm afraid.<br />- However I would liked to of seen more of the Ruined but I think we'll get more in the next two books, and what we did see, I am already very very excited.<br /><br />Overall I'm SO happy I read this, I thought I was getting into a slump but after this I feel greatttt! Thanks Alexis for showing this, because if it wasn't for you I'd never of read it (and also thanks for putting up with many messages). Very very excited to start <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/31371485.Avenged__Ruined___2_" title="Avenged (Ruined, #2) by Amy Tintera" rel="nofollow noopener">Avenged</a>. Also if you're a fan of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22328546.Red_Queen__Red_Queen___1_" title="Red Queen (Red Queen, #1) by Victoria Aveyard" rel="nofollow noopener">Red Queen</a> you may like this!<br /><br />Reviews:<br />Ruined - 5 Stars<br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2511923422" rel="nofollow noopener">Avenged</a> - 3.75 Stars</span>
  <a data-text-id="17595821149990502542" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('gs4kP8pOFcr5qkepkcTAvT4yPgscqqsTVV0Es8tN0fFqP+AZ8IRdBNbiAJ0oj6zgaAJAl0pVFU45I2XM6T8p5g==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('oSzsOJNjfb1AZ82IPn7yF1zbNANbOFP142uJx/AbZOZJ3Sgeqak1c28viryHNZ5KCutKnw3H7aiPFei40mmc8Q==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
